################Opus Dei branch (approve the stabilisation plan)
shared_focus = {
	id = IBR_approve_stabilisation_plan
	icon = GFX_focus_IBR_opus_dei_influence
	cost = 3.00
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = IBR_trust_the_ministries
		focus = IBR_reapply_the_old
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = IBR_asessing_the_economy
	}
	available = {
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = IBR_economic_tree_paths
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = cau_weak_franco
				has_country_flag = cau_council
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = legislature_council
					has_country_flag = cau_weak_salazar
				}
			}
		}
	}
	x = -11
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = IBR_asessing_the_economy
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IBR_approve_stabilisation_plan"
			set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = -3 }
			econ_centralization_change = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				IBR = {
					remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
				}
			}
			add_ideas = IBR_Mariano_Rubio_eco
			IBR_add_5_marklib = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = IBR_iberian_economy_miracle_dyn_mod } 
				set_variable = { IBR_free_prod_units_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_oil_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_power_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_misc_income_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_gdp_growth_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_efficiency_gain_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_capacity_factory_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_building_speed_miracle_variable = 0 }
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.3142
					days = 15
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = legislature_council
				}
				add_to_variable = { IBR_council_reformism = 5 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_stabilisation_plan_tt_1
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
					id = IBR.3123
					hours = 5
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = advisory_council
				}
				add_to_variable = { IBR_council_influence = 5 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_stabilisation_plan_tt_2
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
					id = IBR.3122
					hours = 5
					}
				}
			}
	}
}

	id = IBR_trust_the_ministries
	icon = GFX_focus_IBR_trust_the_ministries
	cost = 3.00
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = IBR_approve_stabilisation_plan
		focus = IBR_reapply_the_old
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = IBR_asessing_the_economy
	}
	available = {
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = IBR_economic_tree_paths
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = cau_strong_salazar
				has_country_flag = cau_weak_salazar
				has_country_flag = cau_council
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = legislature_council
					has_country_flag = cau_weak_franco
				}
			}
		}
	}
	x = 0
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = IBR_asessing_the_economy
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IBR_trust_the_ministries"
		set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = -2 }
		econ_centralization_change = yes
		hidden_effect = {
				IBR = {
					remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
				}
			}
			add_ideas = IBR_Ulisses_Cortes_eco
			IBR_add_5_soccon = yes
			IBR_add_3_soclib = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = IBR_iberian_economy_miracle_dyn_mod } 
				set_variable = { IBR_free_prod_units_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_oil_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_power_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_misc_income_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_gdp_growth_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_efficiency_gain_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_capacity_factory_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_building_speed_miracle_variable = 0 }
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.3142
					days = 15
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = advisory_council
					}
					country_event = {
					id = IBR.3124
					hours = 5
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = legislature_council
					}
					country_event = {
					id = IBR.3125
					hours = 5
					}
				}
			}
	}
}

	id = IBR_a_national_expansion
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_good_economy
	available = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = IBR_corporatist_crisis_flag
		}
	}
	cost = 5.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = IBR_reapply_the_old
		focus = IBR_trust_the_ministries
	}
	x = 6
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = IBR_trust_the_ministries
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IBR_a_national_expansion"
		IBR_improve_business_opinion = yes
		IBR_improve_majority_opinion = yes
		IBR_improve_burocrats_opinion = yes
		add_political_power = -75
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = IBR_national_infrastrcture_plan
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_modernize_the_infrastructures
	cost = 5.00

		focus = IBR_expand_heavy_industry
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = IBR_prospect_new_mines
	}

		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = IBR_corporatist_crisis_flag
		}
	}
	x = 0

	relative_position_id = IBR_a_national_expansion

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IBR_national_infrastrcture_plan"
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.25 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					air_base > 1
					is_on_continent = europe
				}

					instant_build = yes

					state_population_k > 700

				level = 1
				build_only_on_allied = yes
				controller_priority = {
					base = 1

					modifier = {
						tag = IBR
						add = 2
					}
				}
				path = { 1048 4135 15113 }
			}
			build_railway = {
				level = 1
				build_only_on_allied = yes
				controller_priority = {
					base = 1

					modifier = {

						add = 2

###################Autarky branch (Reapply the old)
shared_focus = {
	id = IBR_reapply_the_old
	icon = GFX_focus_IBR_reapply_the_old
	cost = 3.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = IBR_asessing_the_economy
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = IBR_approve_stabilisation_plan
		focus = IBR_trust_the_ministries
	}
	available = {
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = IBR_economic_tree_paths
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = cau_strong_franco
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = advisory_council
					has_country_flag = cau_weak_franco
				}
			}
		}
	}
	x = 11
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = IBR_asessing_the_economy
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IBR_reapply_the_old"
		hidden_effect = {
				IBR = {
					remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
				}
			}
		add_ideas = IBR_Jose_Giron_Velasco_eco
			IBR_add_15_authdem = yes
			set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = 3 }
			econ_centralization_change = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = IBR_iberian_economy_miracle_dyn_mod } 
				set_variable = { IBR_free_prod_units_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_oil_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_power_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_misc_income_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_gdp_growth_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_efficiency_gain_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_capacity_factory_miracle_variable = 0 }
				set_variable = { IBR_building_speed_miracle_variable = 0 }
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.4112
					days = 70
				}
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.4116
					days = 60
				}
			}
			if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = legislature_council
			}
			add_to_variable = { IBR_council_reformism = -5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_reformist_tt_econ_3
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.3127
					hours = 5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = advisory_council
				}
				add_to_variable = { IBR_council_influence = -3 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_influence_tt_econ_3
				hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.3126
					hours = 5
					}
				}
			}
			IBR_council_clamp = yes
	}
}

			add_idea = IBR_choose_carefully_2
		}

		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {
					check_variable = {

					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.1023
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { IBRIberiaStability < 8 }
						check_variable = { IBRIberiaStability > 0.9 }
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = IBRElectionsYES
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_divorce_decision_tt
				set_country_flag = IBR_divorce_decision_flag
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = IBR.4059
						days = 7
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

						}

				}

					id = IBR.5427
					days = 4
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = IBR_oilcrisis_right_1
		clr_country_flag = IBR_oilcrisis_right_2
		clr_country_flag = IBR_oilcrisis_right_3

					days = 3

			limit = {

			clr_country_flag = IBR_ac_social_window_weak

shared_focus = {
	id = IBR_Operation_Don_Henrique
	icon = GFX_focus_IBR_operation_don_henrique
	x = 24
	y = 8
	prerequisite = {
		focus = IBR_Prepare_the_Strike
	}
	available = {
		has_global_flag = algeria_crisis
	}
	cost = 0.75
	will_lead_to_war_with = ILG
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus IBR_Operation_Don_Henrique"

		set_temp_variable = { target = SLG }
		set_temp_variable = { to_add = 5 }
		TNO_add_num_volunteers = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { ITA = { has_country_flag = ITA_Algeria_War_Path } }

				ITA = {
					set_temp_variable = { target = ILG }
					set_temp_variable = { to_add = 4 }
					TNO_add_num_volunteers = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				ITA = {
					set_temp_variable = { target = ILG }
					set_temp_variable = { to_add = 3 }
					TNO_add_num_volunteers = yes
				}
			}
			ITA = { clr_country_flag = ITA_Algeria_War_Path }
			clr_country_flag = IBR_Algeria_War_Path
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ILG
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SLG
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = { id = empiremanagement_ILG.4 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		SLG = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ILG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = algeria_crisis
		set_global_flag = algeria_war

		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.915
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
